Complete Graph Adjacency weight List of the rules and their corresponding transitions.
Sample:
	if  Element[i][j] == 3 then:
		the string binary(i) goes to string binary(j) in 3 steps.
		i.e. there are 2 hidden layers between i and j tarversal on the
		application of the rule [R].
